DECLARE
  trans_id NUMBER(20, 0);
BEGIN
  ee_get_transaction_id(trans_id);
  UPDATE ee_transactions SET commit_id = enif_commitid_seq.nextval, commit_ts = systimestamp
  WHERE id = trans_id;
END;
/

commit;

SET DEFINE OFF;
/


-- takto umožníme nastavování sloupců typu date a number
ALTER SESSION SET NLS_DATE_FORMAT = 'YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS';
ALTER SESSION SET NLS_NUMERIC_CHARACTERS = '. ';
/

  WHERE id = trans_id;

ALTER SESSION SET NLS_DATE_FORMAT = 'YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS';
ALTER SESSION SET NLS_NUMERIC_CHARACTERS = '. ';

-- 1: tabulky;
ALTER TABLE "GAS_PREDDISTRIBUTION_GAS" MODIFY ("A_CORRELATIONSYSTEMFLOW_DB" NUMBER(1, 0));
ALTER TABLE "GAS_PREDDISTRIBUTION_GAS_C" MODIFY ("A_CORRELATIONSYSTEMFLOW_DB" NUMBER(1, 0));
ALTER TABLE "GAS_REPSECURSTDSUPPLYDET" ADD ("PDTNAME" VARCHAR2(120 Char));
ALTER TABLE "GAS_REPSECURSTDSUPPLYDET_C" ADD ("PDTNAME" VARCHAR2(120 Char));
ALTER TABLE "GAS_REPSECURSTDSUPPLYDET" ADD ("TDDNAME" VARCHAR2(10 Char));
ALTER TABLE "GAS_REPSECURSTDSUPPLYDET_C" ADD ("TDDNAME" VARCHAR2(10 Char));
ALTER TABLE "GAS_BSD" ADD ("ROLE" NUMBER(1, 0));
ALTER TABLE "GAS_BSD_C" ADD ("ROLE" NUMBER(1, 0));
ALTER TABLE "GAS_BSD" MODIFY ("RESULT" CLOB);
ALTER TABLE "GAS_BSD_C" MODIFY ("RESULT" CLOB);
-- 2: triggery a pohledy;

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER "GAS_PREDDISTRIBUTION_GAS_U"
BEFORE INSERT OR UPDATE ON "GAS_PREDDISTRIBUTION_GAS"
FOR EACH ROW
DECLARE
	trans_id number;
BEGIN
	ee_get_transaction_id(trans_id);
	:new.EE_TRANS_ID := trans_id;
	INSERT INTO "GAS_PREDDISTRIBUTION_GAS_C" t1(EE_CHANGE_ID, "EE_ITEM_ID", EE_CHANGE_TYPE, EE_TRANS_ID, t1."A_CORRELATIONSYSTEMFLOW_DB", t1."A_DOMINANTDIST_DB", t1."A_LASTMEASURE_DB", t1."CAPTION", t1."DISTRIBUTION_GASFK", t1."EXTERNALID", t1."NAME", t1."PARENTPREDDISTRIBUTION_GASFK", t1."PREDICTION_GASFK", t1."SYS_VER")
	VALUES ("GAS_PREDDISTRIBUTION_GAS_S".nextval, :new."ID", 'u', trans_id, :new."A_CORRELATIONSYSTEMFLOW_DB", :new."A_DOMINANTDIST_DB", :new."A_LASTMEASURE_DB", :new."CAPTION", :new."DISTRIBUTION_GASFK", :new."EXTERNALID", :new."NAME", :new."PARENTPREDDISTRIBUTION_GASFK", :new."PREDICTION_GASFK", :new."SYS_VER");
END;
/

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER "GAS_PREDDISTRIBUTION_GAS_D"
BEFORE DELETE ON "GAS_PREDDISTRIBUTION_GAS"
FOR EACH ROW
DECLARE
	trans_id number;
BEGIN
	ee_get_transaction_id(trans_id);
	INSERT INTO "GAS_PREDDISTRIBUTION_GAS_C"(EE_CHANGE_ID, "EE_ITEM_ID", EE_CHANGE_TYPE, EE_TRANS_ID)
	VALUES ("GAS_PREDDISTRIBUTION_GAS_S".nextval, :old."ID", 'd', trans_id);
END;
/
						
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW "GAS_PREDDISTRIBUTION_GAS_H" AS
SELECT t1."EE_ITEM_ID" "ID", t1.EE_TRANS_ID EE_TRANS_ID, t1."A_CORRELATIONSYSTEMFLOW_DB", t1."A_DOMINANTDIST_DB", t1."A_LASTMEASURE_DB", t1."CAPTION", t1."DISTRIBUTION_GASFK", t1."EXTERNALID", t1."NAME", t1."PARENTPREDDISTRIBUTION_GASFK", t1."PREDICTION_GASFK", t1."SYS_VER"
FROM
"GAS_PREDDISTRIBUTION_GAS_C" t1,
(SELECT EE_ITEM_ID, MAX(EE_CHANGE_ID) KEEP (DENSE_RANK FIRST ORDER BY COMMIT_ID desc, EE_CHANGE_ID desc) trans_change_id
  FROM "GAS_PREDDISTRIBUTION_GAS_C" ti INNER JOIN ee_visible_transactions v ON EE_TRANS_ID = v.id
  GROUP BY EE_ITEM_ID) g
WHERE t1.EE_ITEM_ID=g.EE_ITEM_ID and t1.EE_CHANGE_ID=g.trans_change_id and t1.EE_CHANGE_TYPE <> 'd';
/

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER "GAS_PREDDISTRIBUTION_GAS_HU"
INSTEAD OF UPDATE 
ON "GAS_PREDDISTRIBUTION_GAS_H"
FOR EACH ROW
DECLARE
  ex_nonupdatable EXCEPTION;
	PRAGMA EXCEPTION_INIT( ex_nonupdatable, -20001);
BEGIN
	UPDATE "GAS_PREDDISTRIBUTION_GAS"
	SET "A_CORRELATIONSYSTEMFLOW_DB" = :new."A_CORRELATIONSYSTEMFLOW_DB", "A_DOMINANTDIST_DB" = :new."A_DOMINANTDIST_DB", "A_LASTMEASURE_DB" = :new."A_LASTMEASURE_DB", "CAPTION" = :new."CAPTION", "DISTRIBUTION_GASFK" = :new."DISTRIBUTION_GASFK", "EXTERNALID" = :new."EXTERNALID", "NAME" = :new."NAME", "PARENTPREDDISTRIBUTION_GASFK" = :new."PARENTPREDDISTRIBUTION_GASFK", "PREDICTION_GASFK" = :new."PREDICTION_GASFK", "SYS_VER" = :new."SYS_VER"
	WHERE "ID" = :new."ID" AND EE_TRANS_ID = :new.EE_TRANS_ID;
	IF sql%rowcount <> 1 THEN
		raise_application_error(-20001, 'Pokus o update neplatného řádku, pokud chcete zapisovat do tohoto řádku, načtěte novou verzi dat');
	END IF;
END;
/

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER "GAS_REPSECURSTDSUPPLYDET_U"
BEFORE INSERT OR UPDATE ON "GAS_REPSECURSTDSUPPLYDET"
FOR EACH ROW
DECLARE
	trans_id number;
BEGIN
	ee_get_transaction_id(trans_id);
	:new.EE_TRANS_ID := trans_id;
	INSERT INTO "GAS_REPSECURSTDSUPPLYDET_C" t1(EE_CHANGE_ID, "EE_ITEM_ID", EE_CHANGE_TYPE, EE_TRANS_ID, t1."EMERGENCYCATEGORY", t1."IDPDT", t1."METERINGCAPTION", t1."PDTID", t1."PDTNAME", t1."R30DAYS", t1."REDUNDANCY", t1."REPSECURSTDSUPPLYFK", t1."RMAXDAY", t1."TDDNAME", t1."SYS_VER")
	VALUES ("GAS_REPSECURSTDSUPPLYDET_S".nextval, :new."ID", 'u', trans_id, :new."EMERGENCYCATEGORY", :new."IDPDT", :new."METERINGCAPTION", :new."PDTID", :new."PDTNAME", :new."R30DAYS", :new."REDUNDANCY", :new."REPSECURSTDSUPPLYFK", :new."RMAXDAY", :new."TDDNAME", :new."SYS_VER");
END;
/

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER "GAS_REPSECURSTDSUPPLYDET_D"
BEFORE DELETE ON "GAS_REPSECURSTDSUPPLYDET"
FOR EACH ROW
DECLARE
	trans_id number;
BEGIN
	ee_get_transaction_id(trans_id);
	INSERT INTO "GAS_REPSECURSTDSUPPLYDET_C"(EE_CHANGE_ID, "EE_ITEM_ID", EE_CHANGE_TYPE, EE_TRANS_ID)
	VALUES ("GAS_REPSECURSTDSUPPLYDET_S".nextval, :old."ID", 'd', trans_id);
END;
/
						
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW "GAS_REPSECURSTDSUPPLYDET_H" AS
SELECT t1."EE_ITEM_ID" "ID", t1.EE_TRANS_ID EE_TRANS_ID, t1."EMERGENCYCATEGORY", t1."IDPDT", t1."METERINGCAPTION", t1."PDTID", t1."PDTNAME", t1."R30DAYS", t1."REDUNDANCY", t1."REPSECURSTDSUPPLYFK", t1."RMAXDAY", t1."TDDNAME", t1."SYS_VER"
FROM
"GAS_REPSECURSTDSUPPLYDET_C" t1,
(SELECT EE_ITEM_ID, MAX(EE_CHANGE_ID) KEEP (DENSE_RANK FIRST ORDER BY COMMIT_ID desc, EE_CHANGE_ID desc) trans_change_id
  FROM "GAS_REPSECURSTDSUPPLYDET_C" ti INNER JOIN ee_visible_transactions v ON EE_TRANS_ID = v.id
  GROUP BY EE_ITEM_ID) g
WHERE t1.EE_ITEM_ID=g.EE_ITEM_ID and t1.EE_CHANGE_ID=g.trans_change_id and t1.EE_CHANGE_TYPE <> 'd';
/

	WHERE "ID" = :new."ID" AND EE_TRANS_ID = :new.EE_TRANS_ID;
	IF sql%rowcount <> 1 THEN
		raise_application_error(-20001, 'Pokus o update neplatného řádku, pokud chcete zapisovat do tohoto řádku, načtěte novou verzi dat');

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER "GAS_BSD_U"
BEFORE INSERT OR UPDATE ON "GAS_BSD"
FOR EACH ROW
DECLARE
	trans_id number;
BEGIN
	ee_get_transaction_id(trans_id);
	:new.EE_TRANS_ID := trans_id;
	INSERT INTO "GAS_BSD_C" t1(EE_CHANGE_ID, "EE_ITEM_ID", EE_CHANGE_TYPE, EE_TRANS_ID, t1."DATECREATED", t1."DATEFINISHED", t1."DATESTARTED", t1."PERIODFROM", t1."PERIODTO", t1."PREDICTIONFK", t1."RESULT", t1."ROLE", t1."STATEFK", t1."VERSION", t1."SYS_VER")
	VALUES ("GAS_BSD_S".nextval, :new."ID", 'u', trans_id, :new."DATECREATED", :new."DATEFINISHED", :new."DATESTARTED", :new."PERIODFROM", :new."PERIODTO", :new."PREDICTIONFK", :new."RESULT", :new."ROLE", :new."STATEFK", :new."VERSION", :new."SYS_VER");
END;
/

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER "GAS_BSD_D"
BEFORE DELETE ON "GAS_BSD"
FOR EACH ROW
DECLARE
	trans_id number;
BEGIN
	ee_get_transaction_id(trans_id);
	INSERT INTO "GAS_BSD_C"(EE_CHANGE_ID, "EE_ITEM_ID", EE_CHANGE_TYPE, EE_TRANS_ID)
	VALUES ("GAS_BSD_S".nextval, :old."ID", 'd', trans_id);
END;
/
						
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW "GAS_BSD_H" AS
SELECT t1."EE_ITEM_ID" "ID", t1.EE_TRANS_ID EE_TRANS_ID, t1."DATECREATED", t1."DATEFINISHED", t1."DATESTARTED", t1."PERIODFROM", t1."PERIODTO", t1."PREDICTIONFK", t1."RESULT", t1."ROLE", t1."STATEFK", t1."VERSION", t1."SYS_VER"
FROM
"GAS_BSD_C" t1,
(SELECT EE_ITEM_ID, MAX(EE_CHANGE_ID) KEEP (DENSE_RANK FIRST ORDER BY COMMIT_ID desc, EE_CHANGE_ID desc) trans_change_id
  FROM "GAS_BSD_C" ti INNER JOIN ee_visible_transactions v ON EE_TRANS_ID = v.id
  GROUP BY EE_ITEM_ID) g
WHERE t1.EE_ITEM_ID=g.EE_ITEM_ID and t1.EE_CHANGE_ID=g.trans_change_id and t1.EE_CHANGE_TYPE <> 'd';
/

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER "GAS_BSD_HU"
INSTEAD OF UPDATE 
ON "GAS_BSD_H"
FOR EACH ROW

  ex_nonupdatable EXCEPTION;
	PRAGMA EXCEPTION_INIT( ex_nonupdatable, -20001);

	SET "DATECREATED" = :new."DATECREATED", "DATEFINISHED" = :new."DATEFINISHED", "DATESTARTED" = :new."DATESTARTED", "PERIODFROM" = :new."PERIODFROM", "PERIODTO" = :new."PERIODTO", "PREDICTIONFK" = :new."PREDICTIONFK", "RESULT" = :new."RESULT", "ROLE" = :new."ROLE", "STATEFK" = :new."STATEFK", "VERSION" = :new."VERSION", "SYS_VER" = :new."SYS_VER"
	WHERE "ID" = :new."ID" AND EE_TRANS_ID = :new.EE_TRANS_ID;
	IF sql%rowcount <> 1 THEN
		raise_application_error(-20001, 'Pokus o update neplatného řádku, pokud chcete zapisovat do tohoto řádku, načtěte novou verzi dat');
	END IF;
END;
/

INSTEAD OF DELETE
ON "GAS_BSD_H"
FOR EACH ROW
DECLARE
  ex_nonupdatable EXCEPTION;
	PRAGMA EXCEPTION_INIT( ex_nonupdatable, -20001);
BEGIN
	DELETE FROM "GAS_BSD"
	WHERE "ID" = :old."ID" AND EE_TRANS_ID = :old.EE_TRANS_ID;
	IF sql%rowcount <> 1 THEN
		raise_application_error(-20001, 'Pokus o update neplatného řádku, pokud chcete zapisovat do tohoto řádku, načtěte novou verzi dat');
	END IF;
END;
/
-- 3: závislé objekty (lokalizace);
-- 4: číselníky;
UPDATE "GAS_WFSTATE" SET "CAPTION" = 'Připraveno', "DESCRIPTION" = 'Akce připravena ke spuštění', "KEY" = 'READY', "SHORTCAPTION" = 'Připr.' WHERE "ID" = '1'/
UPDATE "GAS_WFSTATE" SET "CAPTION" = 'Spuštěno', "DESCRIPTION" = 'Akce byla spuštěna', "KEY" = 'RUNNING', "SHORTCAPTION" = 'Spuštěno' WHERE "ID" = '2'/
UPDATE "GAS_WFSTATE" SET "CAPTION" = 'Chyba', "DESCRIPTION" = 'Při běhu akce se vyskytla chyba', "KEY" = 'ERR', "SHORTCAPTION" = 'Chyba' WHERE "ID" = '3'/
UPDATE "GAS_WFSTATE" SET "CAPTION" = 'Dokončeno', "DESCRIPTION" = 'Akce doběhla úspěšně bez chyb', "KEY" = 'DONE', "SHORTCAPTION" = 'Dokonč.' WHERE "ID" = '4'/
UPDATE "GAS_CONSVARIANT_GAS" SET "KEY" = 'heat', "CAPTION" = 'vytápění', "SHORTCAPTION" = 'vytápění', "DESCRIPTION" = 'vytápění', "EXTERNALID" = '2' WHERE "ID" = '2'/
UPDATE "GAS_PREDZONE_GAS" SET "PREDICTION_GASFK" = '1', "DISTRIBUTION_GASFK" = '100001', "CAPTION" = 'Celá ČR', "A_ZONEAGGREGATEALL_DB" = '1', "A_ISVIRTUAL_DB" = '0' WHERE "ID" = '1'/
UPDATE "GAS_PREDZONE_GAS" SET "PREDICTION_GASFK" = '1', "DISTRIBUTION_GASFK" = '100001', "CAPTION" = 'Celá ČR virtual', "A_ZONEAGGREGATEALL_DB" = '0', "A_ISVIRTUAL_DB" = '1' WHERE "ID" = '2'/
UPDATE "GAS_PREDZONE_GAS" SET "PREDICTION_GASFK" = '2', "DISTRIBUTION_GASFK" = '100001', "CAPTION" = 'Celá ČR', "A_ZONEAGGREGATEALL_DB" = '1', "A_ISVIRTUAL_DB" = '0' WHERE "ID" = '3'/
UPDATE "GAS_PREDZONE_GAS" SET "PREDICTION_GASFK" = '2', "DISTRIBUTION_GASFK" = '100001', "CAPTION" = 'Celá ČR virtual', "A_ZONEAGGREGATEALL_DB" = '0', "A_ISVIRTUAL_DB" = '1' WHERE "ID" = '4'/

DECLARE
  trans_id NUMBER(20, 0);
BEGIN
  ee_get_transaction_id(trans_id);
  UPDATE ee_transactions SET commit_id = enif_commitid_seq.nextval, commit_ts = systimestamp
  WHERE id = trans_id;
END;
/

commit;
